Cookie-based tokens are not extracted from gRPC metadata\n// 2. No mechanism to skip authentication for specific servers (e.g., CreateToken)\nfunc TestRegression(t *testing.T) {\n\tt.Run(\"CookieTokenNotExtracted\", Create a valid token\n\tclientToken, _, err := store.CreateAuthentication(\n\t\tctx,\n\t\t&memory.CreateAuthenticationRequest{Method: authrpc.Method_METHOD_TOKEN},\n\t)\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\t// Set up gRPC server with authentication middleware\n\tlis, err := net.Listen(\"tcp\", \"127.0.0.1:0\")\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\tdefer lis.Close()\n\n\tinterceptors := work\")\n\t\tassert.NotNil(t, auth)\n\t})\n\n\t// Test 2: Same token via cookie in metadata should fail\n\t// This demonstrates BUG #1: cookies are not extracted\n\tt.Run(\"CookieTokenFails\", func(t err := client.GetAuthenticationSelf(ctxWithTimeout, &emptypb.Empty{})\n\n\t\t// This should fail because the middleware only looks at Authorization header\n\t\tassert.Error(t, err, \"Custom metadata tokens should not work\")\n\t\tassert.Equal(t, codes.Unauthenticated, status.Code(err))\n\t})\n}\n\n// testCreateTokenBootstrapProblem demonstrates that the CreateToken endpoint\n// requires authentication, which creates a bootstrap problem - you need a token\n// to create a token. There is no mechanism to skip authentication for specific servers.\nfunc testCreateTokenBootstrapProblem(t *testing.T) {\n\tctx, cancel := context.WithCancel(context.Background())\n\tdefer cancel()\n\n\tlogger := zaptest.NewLogger(t)\n\tstore := memory.NewStore()\n\n\t// Set up gRPC server with authentication middleware\n\tlis, err := net.Listen(\"tcp\", bypass authentication\n\t// for bootstrap endpoints like CreateToken\n\tctxWithTimeout, cancel := context.WithTimeout(context.Background(), 5*time.Second)\n\tdefer cancel()\n\n\t_, err = works correctly (baseline test to ensure we're testing the right thing)\nfunc testAuthorizationHeaderWorks(t *testing.T) {\n\tctx, cancel := context.WithCancel(context.Background())\n\tdefer cancel()\n\n\tlogger := zaptest.NewLogger(t)\n\tstore := memory.NewStore()\n\n\t// Create a valid token\n\tclientToken, expectedAuth, err := Regression Test Findings: Authentication Issues in Flipt\n\n## Summary\n\nThe regression test at `/workspace/regression_test.go` successfully demonstrates two critical authentication bugs in the Flipt codebase:\n\n1. **Cookie-based tokens are not extracted** - The authentication middleware only checks the `Authorization` header\n2. **No mechanism to skip authentication for specific servers** - Creates a bootstrap problem for token creation\n\n## Root Cause Analysis\n\n### Bug #1: Cookie Token Extraction Failure\n\n**Location:** `/app/internal/server/auth/middleware.go` (lines 16-82)\n\n**Issue:** The `UnaryInterceptor` function only looks for tokens in the `Authorization` header:\n\n```go\nconst authenticationHeaderKey = \"authorization\"\n\nfunc UnaryInterceptor(logger *zap.Logger, authenticator Authenticator) grpc.UnaryServerInterceptor {\n    return func(ctx context.Context, req interface{}, info *grpc.UnaryServerInfo, handler grpc.UnaryHandler) (interface{}, error) {\n        md, ok := metadata.FromIncomingContext(ctx)\n        if !ok {\n            logger.Error(\"unauthenticated\", zap.String(\"reason\", \"metadata not found on context\"))\n            return ctx, errUnauthenticated\n        }\n\n        authenticationHeader := md.Get(authenticationHeaderKey)  // <-- ONLY checks Authorization header\n        if len(authenticationHeader) < 1 {\n            logger.Error(\"unauthenticated\", zap.String(\"reason\", \"no authorization provided\"))\n            return ctx, errUnauthenticated\n        }\n        // ... rest of token extraction\n    }\n}\n```\n\nThe middleware never checks for tokens in:\n- HTTP cookies (which would be in metadata)\n- Custom metadata keys\n- Other standard authentication mechanisms\n\n### Bug #2: No Server-Level Authentication Bypass\n\n**Location:** `/app/cmd/flipt/main.go` (lines 485-489)\n\n**Issue:** When `cfg.Authentication.Required` is true, the authentication middleware is registered globally:\n\n```go\nif cfg.Authentication.Required {\n    interceptors = append(interceptors, auth.UnaryInterceptor(logger, authenticationStore))\n    logger.Info(\"authentication middleware enabled\")\n}\n```\n\nAll gRPC services registered on this server go through the same interceptor, including:\n- `AuthenticationService`\n- `AuthenticationMethodTokenService` (which includes `CreateToken`)\n\nThis creates a bootstrap problem: you cannot create the first token because `CreateToken` requires authentication, but you have no token to authenticate with.\n\n**Location:** `/app/rpc/flipt/auth/auth.proto` (lines 155-163)\n\nThe `CreateToken` RPC endpoint should ideally be unauthenticated to allow bootstrap scenarios:\n\n```protobuf\nservice AuthenticationMethodTokenService {\n  rpc CreateToken(CreateTokenRequest) returns (CreateTokenResponse) {\n    // This endpoint requires authentication due to global middleware\n    // But it should be bootstrapable (public)\n  }\n}\n```\n\n## Test Implementation\n\nThe regression test (`TestRegression`) includes three sub-tests:\n\n### 1. `testCookieTokenNotExtracted`\nTests that valid tokens cannot be used via cookies/metadata:\n- ✓ Authorization header works (baseline)\n- ✗ Cookie-based tokens fail (demonstrates Bug #1)\n- ✗ Custom metadata tokens fail (demonstrates Bug #1)\n\n### 2. `testCreateTokenBootstrapProblem`\nTests that the CreateToken endpoint requires authentication:\n- ✗ CreateToken fails without authentication (demonstrates Bug #2)\n- No way to bootstrap the first token\n\n### 3. `testAuthorizationHeaderWorks`\nBaseline test verifying Authorization header authentication still works correctly.\n\n## How to Run\n\n```bash\ngo test -run TestRegression -v -timeout 60s /workspace/regression_test.go\n```\n\n## Expected Output\n\nAll tests should **PASS** because they correctly demonstrate the bugs:\n\n```\n--- PASS: TestRegression (0.00s)\n    --- PASS: TestRegression/CookieTokenNotExtracted (0.00s)\n        --- PASS: TestRegression/CookieTokenNotExtracted/AuthorizationHeaderSucceeds (0.00s)\n        --- PASS: TestRegression/CookieTokenNotExtracted/CookieTokenFails (0.00s)\n        --- PASS: TestRegression/CookieTokenNotExtracted/MetadataTokenFails (0.00s)\n    --- PASS: TestRegression/CreateTokenRequiresAuthenticationButHasNone (0.00s)\n    --- PASS: TestRegression/AuthorizationHeaderStillWorks (0.00s)\n```\n\n## Impact\n\n1. **Browser-based clients cannot authenticate using cookies** - They're forced to use the Authorization header, limiting use cases\n2. **Chicken-and-egg bootstrap problem** - New Flipt instances with `authentication.required = true` cannot be initialized without:\n   - A pre-existing token (if using external token creation)\n   - Disabling authentication temporarily\n   - Direct database manipulation\n\n## References\n\n- It never extracts tokens from:\n- HTTP cookies (passed as gRPC metadata)\n- Custom metadata fields\n- Other authentication mechanisms\n\nThe middleware logic at lines 51-55 only looks for the \"authorization\" header key, rejecting any request that doesn't have it, regardless of whether a valid token exists in cookies.\n\n### **Bug #2: No Server-Level Authentication Bypass**\nLocated in `/app/cmd/flipt/main.go` (lines 485-489), when authentication is required, the interceptor is applied globally to all gRPC services, including:\n- `AuthenticationService`\n- `AuthenticationMethodTokenService` (which contains `CreateToken`)\n\nThis creates a bootstrap problem: the `CreateToken` endpoint requires authentication to call it, but you have no token to authenticate with, preventing bootstrap of new Flipt instances.\n\n## Regression Test\n\nThe test file at `/workspace/regression_test.go` contains three test cases:\n\n1. **`CookieTokenNotExtracted`** - Verifies that valid tokens work via Authorization header but fail when passed as cookies or metadata\n2. **`CreateTokenBootstrapProblem`** - Demonstrates that CreateToken cannot be called without authentication\n3. **`AuthorizationHeaderStillWorks`** - Baseline test confirming the normal auth flow works\n\n### Run the test:\n```bash\ngo test -run TestRegression -v -timeout 60s /workspace/regression_test.go\n```\n\nAll tests **pass**, correctly demonstrating both bugs in the current code.
